Overview\\nThe CRD (CustomResourceDefinition) validation schema to OpenAPI conversion pipeline in Kubernetes involves multiple stages of transformation and publication. The flow begins with the CRD validation specification and ends with published OpenAPI v2 and v3 endpoints on the Kubernetes API server.\\n\\n### Stage 1: CRD Validation Specification\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types_jsonschema.go`\\n\\nThe CRD validation schema is defined using `JSONSchemaProps` struct, which follows JSON Schema Draft 4 specification. This struct contains all validation rules including:\\n- Type information (Type field)\\n- Constraint fields (Pattern, MaxLength, MinLength, etc.)\\n- Composition fields (AllOf, AnyOf, OneOf, Not)\\n- Kubernetes-specific extensions (XPreserveUnknownFields, XIntOrString, etc.)\\n- Default values and required field lists\\n\\n### Stage 2: Structural Schema Extraction\\n**Files**:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go` - Defines the Structural schema type\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/convert.go` - Contains `NewStructural()` function\\n\\nThe `NewStructural()` function (in convert.go:42) converts the JSONSchemaProps into a more constrained \\\"Structural\\\" schema representation. The Structural type:\\n- Preserves the schema structure (Items, Properties, AdditionalProperties)\\n- Separates concerns into Generic (type, description, title, default, nullable), Extensions (Kubernetes-specific x- fields), ValidationExtensions (x-kubernetes-validations), and ValueValidation (constraint and composition fields)\\n- Validates that the schema meets structural invariants (no $ref, patternProperties, additionalItems, etc.)\\n- This intermediate representation is critical for ensuring schemas are compatible with kubectl and other client tools\\n\\n### Stage 3: Schema Transformation and Unfolding\\n**Files**:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/unfold.go` - `Unfold()` method\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/skeleton.go` - `StripValueValidations()` and `StripNullable()` methods\\n\\nAfter structural conversion, the schema undergoes optional transformations:\\n- `Unfold()` expands vendor extensions like x-kubernetes-int-or-string into explicit AnyOf patterns\\n- `StripValueValidations()` removes composition operators (AllOf, AnyOf, OneOf, Not) when needed\\n- `StripNullable()` removes nullable properties when needed for OpenAPI v2 compatibility\\n\\nThese transformations are recorded in the ValueValidation structure to maintain semantic fidelity.\\n\\n### Stage 4: OpenAPI v3 Schema Conversion\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/kubeopenapi.go`\\n\\nThe `ToKubeOpenAPI()` method (kubeopenapi.go:24) converts the Structural schema to a go-openapi schema (spec.Schema). This conversion:\\n- Maps Structural fields to spec.Schema fields\\n- Recursively converts nested Items and Properties\\n- Preserves all Kubernetes extensions via vendor extensions (x-kubernetes-* fields)\\n- Handles AdditionalProperties appropriately\\n- Converts the Generic fields (type, description, title, default, nullable) to their OpenAPI equivalents\\n- Preserves validation extensions (x-kubernetes-validations for CEL rules)\\n\\n### Stage 5: OpenAPI Builder and Version-Specific Conversion\\n**Files**:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/builder/builder.go` - Contains `BuildOpenAPIV2()` and `BuildOpenAPIV3()` functions\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/v2/conversion.go` - Contains `ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` function\\n\\nThe builder orchestrates the complete conversion process:\\n\\n1. **BuildOpenAPIV2()** (builder.go:204):\\n   - Extracts the structural schema from the CRD version's OpenAPIV3Schema\\n   - Calls `NewStructural()` to convert JSONSchemaProps to Structural\\n   - Calls `Unfold()` to expand vendor extensions\\n   - Optionally strips value validations and nullable fields based on options\\n   - Applies `ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` to remove OpenAPI v3-only features (AllOf, OneOf, AnyOf, Not)\\n   - Converts to go-openapi spec.Schema via `ToKubeOpenAPI()`\\n   -
